Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,This letter was from you. It contained information relative to Clithero.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,See how imminent a chance it was that saved my wife from a knowledge of
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,its contents! It required all my efforts to hide my perturbation from
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,her and excuse myself from showing her the letter.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I know better than you the character of Clithero, and the consequences
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,of a meeting between him and my wife. You may be sure that I would exert
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,myself to prevent a meeting.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,The method for me to pursue was extremely obvious. Clithero is a madman,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,whose liberty is dangerous, and who requires to be fettered and
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,imprisoned as the most atrocious criminal.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I hastened to the chief-magistrate, who is my friend, and, by proper
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,representations, obtained from him authority to seize Clithero wherever
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I should meet with him, and effectually debar him from the perpetration
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,of new mischiefs.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,New York does not afford a place of confinement for lunatics as suitable
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,to his case as Pennsylvania. I was desirous of placing him as far as
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,possible from the place of my wife's residence. Fortunately, there was a
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,packet for Philadelphia on the point of setting out on her voyage. This
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,vessel I engaged to wait a day or two, for the purpose of conveying him
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,to Pennsylvania Hospital. Meanwhile, proper persons were stationed at
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,Powles Hook, and at the quays where the various stage-boats from Jersey
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,arrive.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,These precautions were effectual. Not many hours after the receipt of
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,your intelligence, this unfortunate man applied for a passage at
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,Elizabethtown, was seized the moment he set his foot on shore, and was
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,forthwith conveyed to the packet, which immediately set sail.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I designed that all these proceedings should be concealed from the
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,women, but unfortunately neglected to take suitable measures for
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,hindering the letter, which you gave me reason to expect on the ensuing
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,day, from coming into their hands. It was delivered to my wife in my
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,absence, and opened immediately by her.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,You know what is, at present, her personal condition. You know what
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,strong reasons I had to prevent any danger or alarm from approaching
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,her. Terror could not assume a shape more ghastly than this. The effects
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,have been what might have been easily predicted. Her own life has been
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,imminently endangered, and an untimely birth has blasted my fondest
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,hope. Her infant, with whose future existence so many pleasures were
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,entwined, is dead.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I assure you, Edgar, my philosophy has not found itself lightsome and
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,active under this burden. I find it hard to forbear commenting on your
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,rashness in no very mild terms. You acted in direct opposition to my
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,counsel and to the plainest dictates of propriety. Be more circumspect
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,and more obsequious for the future.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,You knew the liberty that would be taken of opening my letters; you knew
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,of my absence from home during the greatest part of the day, and the
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,likelihood, therefore, that your letters would fall into my wife's hands
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,before they came into mine. These considerations should have prompted
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,you to send them under cover to Whitworth or Harvey, with directions to
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,give them immediately to me.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,Some of these events happened in my absence; for I determined to
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,accompany the packet myself, and see the madman safely delivered to the
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,care of the hospital.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,I will not torture your sensibility by recounting the incidents of his
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,arrest and detention. You will imagine that his strong but perverted
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,reason exclaimed loudly against the injustice of his treatment. It was
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,easy for him to out-reason his antagonist, and nothing but force could
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,subdue his opposition. On me devolved the province of his jailer and his
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,tyrant,--a province which required a heart more steeled by spectacles of
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,suffering and the exercise of cruelty than mine had been.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,Scarcely had we passed the Narrows, when the lunatic, being suffered to
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,walk the deck, (as no apprehensions were entertained of his escape in
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,such circumstances,) threw himself overboard, with a seeming intention
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,to gain the shore. The boat was immediately manned; the fugitive was
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,pursued; but, at the moment when his flight was overtaken, he forced
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,himself beneath the surface, and was seen no more.
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,With the life of this wretch, let our regrets and our forebodings
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,terminate. He has saved himself from evils for which no time would have
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,provided a remedy, from lingering for years in the noisome dungeon of a
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,hospital. Having no reason to continue my voyage, I put myself on board
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,a coasting-sloop, and regained this city in a few hours. I persuade
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,myself that my wife's indisposition will be temporary. It was impossible
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,to hide from her the death of Clithero, and its circumstances. May this
Memoirs-of-a-Sleep-Walker,1880,Huntly-Edgar,be the last arrow in the quiver of adversity! Farewell.
